Assurance, prévention, gestion des contrats et des sinistres, retrouvez tous les services Luko à tout moment, directement dans votre poche ↓Une assurance efficace, personnalisée et sans contrainte :- Accédez aux détails de ce qui est inclus ou non, en un coup d'œil- Assurez-vous en 2 minutes en ligne- Discutez avec notre service clientèle, le meilleur de sa catégorie, tous les jours de la semaine- Téléchargez ou partagez votre attestation d'assurance- Ajoutez des bénéficiaires ou des options en un clic- Résiliez votre contrat sans préavisDes sinistres gérés en un éclair, sans paperasse ni prise de tête :- Déclarez votre sinistre directement dans l'application, en 5 minutes- Ajoutez des documents, des photos et des vidéos- Accédez à l'état de votre sinistre et aux mises à jour 24 heures sur 24, 7 jours sur 7- Bénéficiez d’un suivi personnalisé avec un gestionnaire dédiéDes couvertures au juste prix, pour assurer ce qui compte pour vous - Assurance emprunteur : couvrez votre prêt immobilier et économisez jusqu'à 15 000 € en passant chez Luko- Assurance habitation : protégez votre foyer et économisez jusqu'à 20% par an- Assurance propriétaire non occupant (PNO) : assurez votre bien locatif en 1 clic- Assurance trottinette électrique : couvrez votre responsabilité civile à partir de 3,50€.et bien d'autres produits à venir !Des services en plus pour gérer votre foyer au quotidien- Un réseau d’artisans de confiance pour confier vos projets de réparation ou de rénovation- Un service de visio pour obtenir des conseils de nos experts du foyer- Une bibliothèque de tutos et astuces pour gérer vos réparations du quotidien- Des alertes météo en cas d'événements climatiques à risqueDate de mise à jour13 déc. 2023FinanceSécurité des donnéesarrow_forwardLa sécurité, c'est d'abord comprendre comment les développeurs collectent et partagent vos données. Title: Luko is hiring, join us! Check out our job opportunities! - Luko

H1: This website uses cookies to ensure you get the best experience on our website. Select which cookies you accept Hello, we are Luko

P: Luko  and selected partners use cookies and similar technologies to ensure you get the best experience on this website.
        If you consent to it, we will use cookies for analytics and marketing purposes. See our Cookie Policy to read more about the cookies we set. You can withdraw and manage your consent at any time, by clicking "Manage cookies" at the bottom of each website page. On this site, we always set cookies that are strictly necessary, meaning they are necessary for the site to function properly. If you consent to it, we will also set other types of cookies. You can provide or withdraw your consent to the different types of cookies using the toggles below. You can change or withdraw your consent at any time, by clicking the link “Manage Cookies”, which is always available at the bottom of the site. To learn more about what the different types of cookies do, how your data is used when they are set etc, see our Cookie Policy. These cookies are necessary to make the site work properly, and are always set when you visit the site. These cookies collect information to help us understand how the site is being used. These cookies are used to make advertising messages more relevant to you. In some cases, they also deliver additional functions on the site.  We created Luko with a simple vision. 50% of consumers don’t trust their insurer, yet it is mandatory in many cases and it is the only stakeholder you can turn to when a damage occurs in your home. So we decided to reinvent insurance to make it finally customer-centric like we believe it was meant to be. We started by creating the most transparent and useful insurance company out there: one that you can finally trust, because its business model was designed for positive impact and because its product experience is meant to empower users rather than mislead them. We created the most intuitive and user-obsessed insurance experience you can wish for: one that you can take out in less than 2 minutes, one that gives you access to an advisor in less than 100 seconds and one that refunds twice faster when you have a damage. In 6 years, we have convinced over 450,000 users to trust us. We rapidly became the online home insurance market, putting technology at the service of customer satisfaction and operational efficiency: by 2022, 25% of home insurance policies sold online in France were Luko policies; and nearly one in two new Luko customers took out a policy on the recommendation of friends and family.  Our generation faces a tremendous number of global challenges and risks. Luko being an insurance company makes it all the more obvious, as we are first faced with most of the climate risks and its impact on building, thus on homes, thus on people. Raphaël Vullierme CEO of Luko Working at Luko is embracing the Luko Way. We strongly believe this set of values defined by the team is what drives us on a daily basis, makes us a united team and helps us deliver a 1% better experience to our users every day. Turns out French people's average mortgage insurance is 15.000 € too expensive for one's profile, so that's why we decided to craft a mortgage insurance that's finally fair. About 1/4 of new Luko users, and even if it's not the majority of them, we're really proud of providing an experience worth recommending for our users. Because honestly... who talks about an insurer if it's not because there's something wrong? Only 50% of French people trust their insurance according to a YouGov survey. Which means the other half is tied to an insurer they don't trust. So that's why we decided to implement the Giveback into our business model, finally realigning interests of everyone.

We created Luko with a simple vision.50% of consumers don’t trust their insurer, yet it is mandatory in many cases and it is the only stakeholder you can turn to when a damage occurs in your home. We rapidly became the online home insurance market, putting technology at the service of customer satisfaction and operational efficiency: by 2022, 25% of home insurance policies sold online in France were Luko policies; and nearly one in two new Luko customers took out a policy on the recommendation of friends and family. Log in to Connect  Hello, we are Luko

Connect Hello, we are Luko

Connect Connect   Our mission? Be your #1 customer centric insurer
We created Luko with a simple vision.50% of consumers don’t trust their insurer, yet it is mandatory in many cases and it is the only stakeholder you can turn to when a damage occurs in your home. So we decided to reinvent insurance to make it finally customer-centric like we believe it was meant to be.We started by creating the most transparent and useful insurance company out there: one that you can finally trust, because its business model was designed for positive impact and because its product experience is meant to empower users rather than mislead them.We created the most intuitive and user-obsessed insurance experience you can wish for: one that you can take out in less than 2 minutes, one that gives you access to an advisor in less than 100 seconds and one that refunds twice faster when you have a damage.In 6 years, we have convinced over 450,000 users to trust us. We rapidly became the online home insurance market, putting technology at the service of customer satisfaction and operational efficiency: by 2022, 25% of home insurance policies sold online in France were Luko policies; and nearly one in two new Luko customers took out a policy on the recommendation of friends and family. Working at Luko is embracing the Luko Way. We strongly believe this set of values defined by the team is what drives us on a daily basis, makes us a united team and helps us deliver a 1% better experience to our users every day. Here’s what it’s like to work at Luko

Learn more about the Luko Way Learn more about the Luko Way  You're here because of our LinkedIn surveys? Here are the latest answers!


      In your opinion, how much do you overpay your mortgage insurance?
      


Turns out French people's average mortgage insurance is 15.000 € too expensive for one's profile, so that's why we decided to craft a mortgage insurance that's finally fair.


      Can you guess how many people get Luko thanks to word of mouth?
      


About 1/4 of new Luko users, and even if it's not the majority of them, we're really proud of providing an experience worth recommending for our users. Because honestly... who talks about an insurer if it's not because there's something wrong?


      How many people actually trust their insurer?
      


Only 50% of French people trust their insurance according to a YouGov survey. Which means the other half is tied to an insurer they don't trust. So that's why we decided to implement the Giveback into our business model, finally realigning interests of everyone. You're here because of our LinkedIn surveys? Here are the latest answers!
